<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="infection-and-pain">Infection and Pain<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#infection-and-pain" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>infection arises from neutropenia (low neutrophils)</li>
<li>people with advanced cancer have pain</li>
<li>severe infection and pain can interfere with the person's ability to enjoy quality life</li>
<li>pain management is the <strong>priority</strong> in care of clients with advanced cancer</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="hypercalcemia">Hypercalcemia<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#hypercalcemia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>due to bone resorption (demineralization)</li>
<li>serum calcium level &gt; 11 mg/dL</li>
<li>usually occurs in <strong>solid tumors</strong> like breast, lung, head, neck and renal CAs</li>
<li>may also occur in <strong>hematologic cancer</strong> like multiple myeloma, leukemia</li>
<li>severe hypercalcemia may lead to:</li>
<li>renal failure</li>
<li>coma</li>
<li>cardiac arrest</li>
<li>death</li>
<li><strong>Calcitonin</strong> (Miacalcin) and oral <strong>glucocorticoids</strong> are given to lower serum calcium</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="tumor-lysis-syndrome">Tumor Lysis Syndrome<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#tumor-lysis-syndrome" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>the destruction of large number of malignant cells may rapidly release intracellular potassium, phosphorous and nucleic acid into the circulation</li>
<li>electrolyte imbalances and acute renal failure may occur</li>
<li>clients with malignancies that are very responsive to treatment are at highest risk especially if they have large tumor burden (lymphomas, leukemias and small cell carcinoma)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="manifestations">MANIFESTATIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#manifestations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Weakness</li>
<li>Nausea</li>
<li>Diarrhea</li>
<li>Flaccid paralysis</li>
<li>ECG changes</li>
<li>Muscle cramps or twitching</li>
<li>Oliguria (&gt;80 ml, &lt;400ml urine output)</li>
<li>Hypotension</li>
<li>Edema</li>
<li>Altered mental status</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="tumor-lysis-syndrome">Tumor Lysis Syndrome<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#tumor-lysis-syndrome" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>collaborative management include the following:</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>Intravenous hydration</li>
<li>Allopurinol to decrease uric acid concentration</li>
<li>Sodium bicarbonate with IV hydration to promote fecal excretion of excess phosphate</li>
<li>Lowering of serum potassium levels with medications, retention enemas, IV 50% dextrose</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="syndrome-of-inappropriate-antidiuretics-hormone">Syndrome of Inappropriate Antidiuretics Hormone<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#syndrome-of-inappropriate-antidiuretics-hormone" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>results from the abnormal production of antidiuretic hormone (ADH)</li>
<li>may be caused by:</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>small cell lung cancer</li>
<li>infection</li>
<li>pulmonary disorders</li>
<li>emotional stress</li>
<li>CNS disorders</li>
<li>some drugs, including antineoplastic agents like Cytoxan (Cyclophosphamide), Oncovin (Vincristine), Velban (Vinblastin), Platinol - AQ (Cisplatin)</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="syndrome-of-inappropriate-antidiuretics-hormone">Syndrome of Inappropriate Antidiuretics Hormone<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#syndrome-of-inappropriate-antidiuretics-hormone" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>manifested by water retention and decrease in sodium</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="signs-and-symptoms">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Confusion</li>
<li>Irritability</li>
<li>Headache</li>
<li>Muscle weakness</li>
<li>Lethargy</li>
<li>Decreased urine output</li>
<li>Edema</li>
<li>Nausea and vomiting</li>
<li>Anorexia</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="syndrome-of-inappropriate-antidiuretics-hormone">Syndrome of Inappropriate Antidiuretics Hormone<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#syndrome-of-inappropriate-antidiuretics-hormone" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>collaborative management are as follows:</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>Fluid excretion (diuretics)</li>
<li>IV infusion of hypertonic saline (3% to 5%) if severe, to prevent pulmonary edema</li>
<li>Monitor intake and output</li>
<li>Administer medications like Declomycine (Demeclocycline), Lithane (Lithium), and urea</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="disseminated-intravascular-coagulation-dic">Disseminated Intravascular Coagulation (DIC)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disseminated-intravascular-coagulation-dic" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>characterized by development of extensive, abnormal clots in the microcirculation (small blood vessels)</li>
<li>widespread clotting depletes the general circulation with clotting factors and platelets leading to excessive bleeding in different sites of the body</li>
<li>clots that are obstructing the circulation decrease blood flow to major organs, causing pain, stroke-like manifestations, dyspnea, tachycardia, oliguna, bowel necrosis</li>
<li>in cancer, usually caused by gram-negative infection or sepsis, release of clotting factors from cancer cells, or blood transfusion</li>
<li>most commonly associated with leukemia and adenocarcinomas of the lung, pancreas, stomach and prostate</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="disseminated-intravascular-coagulation-dic">Disseminated Intravascular Coagulation (DIC)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disseminated-intravascular-coagulation-dic" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>diagnostic findings:</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>prolonged prothrombin time and activated partial thromboplastin time</li>
<li>very low platelet count</li>
<li>prolonged clotting times</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>medical management are as follows:</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>Correction of the basic problem (e.g., infection).</li>
<li>Administer blood products and medication as prescribed</li>
<li>IV heparin if with manifestations of thrombosis (although controversial)</li>
<li>Monitor the client for signs and symptoms of bleeding.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="spinal-cord-compression">Spinal Cord Compression<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#spinal-cord-compression" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>caused by <strong>direct pressure</strong> or <strong>compromise of vascular supply</strong> to the spinal cord</li>
<li><strong>back pain</strong> is often the only presenting clinical manifestation in majority of clients</li>
<li>may result to <strong>irreversible neurologic damage</strong> with paralysis and loss of bowel and bladder control</li>
<li>treatment is usually with RT; laminectomy may be an alternative</li>
<li><strong>steroids</strong> to reduce inflammation and swelling</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="superior-vena-cava-syndrome">Superior Vena Cava Syndrome<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#superior-vena-cava-syndrome" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>results from external and internal obstruction of the superior vena cava</li>
<li>obstruction reduces venous return to the heart and decreases cardiac output</li>
<li>usually secondary to lung cancer or lymphoma</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="clinical-manifestations">CLINICAL MANIFESTATIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#clinical-manifestations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Dyspnea</li>
<li>Facial swelling</li>
<li>Jugular vein distention</li>
<li>Sitting up and leaning forward to breathe</li>
<li>Swelling of arms, chest pain, dysphagia</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>external-beam RT and curative chemotherapy are used for palliation</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cardiac-tamponade">Cardiac Tamponade<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cardiac-tamponade" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>fluid collects in the pericardial sac (pericardial effusion)</li>
<li>pericardiocentesis may be performed to draw off the fluid</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-3b93a853.jpeg" alt="img-96.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="care-of-clients-with-cancer">Care of Clients with Cancer<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#care-of-clients-with-cancer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-e7853b38.jpeg" alt="img-97.jpeg"></p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-174d260a.jpeg" alt="img-98.jpeg"></p>
<p>ASSESSMENT FINDINGS</p>
<ul>
<li>hoarseness of voice (most usual)</li>
<li>mass on anterior neck</li>
<li>dysphagia, burning sensation with hot/acidic beverages</li>
<li>halitosis</li>
<li>hemoptysis</li>
</ul>
<p>COLLABORATIVE MANAGEMENT</p>
<ul>
<li>surgery: laryngectomy</li>
<li>subtotal – retains voice</li>
<li>total – absolute loss of voice</li>
</ul>
<p>CARE OF CLIENTS WITH CANCER OF THE LARYNX</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-5fa0e174.jpeg" alt="img-99.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="laryngectomy">LARYNGECTOMY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#laryngectomy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="preop-care">Preop care<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#preop-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>psychological support</li>
<li>loss of voice</li>
<li>permanent tracheostomy</li>
<li>loss of sense of smell</li>
<li>inability to: blow, blow the nose, sip, whistle, gargle, Valsalva maneuver</li>
<li>establish means of communication to be used post-op</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="care-of-clients-with-cancer-of-the-larynx">CARE OF CLIENTS WITH CANCER OF THE LARYNX<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#care-of-clients-with-cancer-of-the-larynx" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-8b50633a.jpeg" alt="img-100.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client with tracheostomy</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-15dd6a80.jpeg" alt="img-101.jpeg"></p>
<table><thead><tr><th>NURSING CARE</th><th>PROCEDURE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Establish patent airway</td><td>- suction as necessary</td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul>
<li>sterile technique</li>
<li>semi-fowler's position</li>
<li>use NSS to lubricate suction catheter tip</li>
<li>apply suction during withdrawal of suction cath</li>
<li>apply suction for 5-10 secs (max of 15 secs)</li>
<li>insert 3-5 in of the suction cath</li>
<li>instill 2-5 cc NSS to liquefy secretions  |</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client with tracheostomy</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-27102c35.jpeg" alt="img-102.jpeg"></p>
<table><thead><tr><th>NURSING CARE</th><th>PROCEDURE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Prevent infection</td><td>- cleanse stoma and tracheostomy at regular basis</td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul>
<li>change dressings and ties as necessary  |
|  Establish means of communication |   |
|  Psychological support |   |
|  Assist during speech theraophy |   |</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-75cbfa91.jpeg" alt="img-103.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="assessment-findings">ASSESSMENT FINDINGS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#assessment-findings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>cough (hacking, nonproductive initially, then thick, purulent blood-tinged sputum)</li>
<li>pleural effusion</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="collaborative-management">COLLABORATIVE MANAGEMENT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#collaborative-management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>maintain patent airway</li>
<li>administer oxygen and aerosol therapy</li>
<li>DBE</li>
<li>relief of pain</li>
<li>protection from infection</li>
<li>adequate nutrition</li>
<li>chest tube management</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="care-of-clients-with-lung-cancer">CARE OF CLIENTS WITH LUNG CANCER<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#care-of-clients-with-lung-cancer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>surgery:
<strong>PNEUMONECTOMY</strong></li>
<li>removal of a lung</li>
<li>position in semi-fowler’s, turned on affected side (to promote lung expansion, prevent flooding of the remaining lung with blood)</li>
<li>avoid full side-lying position (to prevent mediastinal shift)</li>
<li>no chest tube after surgery
<strong>LOBECTOMY</strong> - removal of a lobe
<strong>SEGMENTECTOMY</strong> - removal of a segment
<strong>WEDGE RESECTION</strong> - removal of an entire tumor regardless of the segment
<strong>DECORTICATION</strong> - stripping off of fibrinous membrane enclosing the lung
<strong>THORACOPLASTY</strong> - removal of ribs, usually done after pneumonectomy (to reduce size of empty thorax, thereby preventing mediastinal shift)</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>CARE OF CLIENTS WITH LUNG CANCER</strong></p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-75cbfa91.jpeg" alt="img-104.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="stages-of-breast-cancer">STAGES OF BREAST CANCER<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stages-of-breast-cancer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="stage-i">Stage I<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stage-i" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Tumor size is up to 2cm.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="stage-ii">Stage II<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stage-ii" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Tumor size is up to 5 cm with axillary lymph node involvement</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="stage-iii">Stage III<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stage-iii" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Tumor size is more than 5 cm., with axillary and neck lymph no involvement</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="stage-iv">Stage IV<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#stage-iv" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>Metastasis to distant organs (liver, lungs, bone and brain)</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="care-of-clients-with-breast-cancer">CARE OF CLIENTS WITH BREAST CANCER<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#care-of-clients-with-breast-cancer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-115e585f.jpeg" alt="img-105.jpeg"></p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-5a044dc2.jpeg" alt="img-106.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="collaborrative-mananagement">COLLABORRATIVE MANANAGEMENT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#collaborrative-mananagement" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="surgery">Surgery<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#surgery" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Lumpectomy/tylectomy - removal of the lump</li>
<li>Simple Mastectomy - removal of the entire breast; pectoralis muscles and the nipple remain intact</li>
<li>Modified Radical Mastectomy (MRM) - removal of the entire breast and the axillary lymph nodes; pectoralis muscles are conserved</li>
<li>Radical Mastectomy (Halstead Surgery) - removal of the entire breast, pectoralis major and minor muscles and the axillary lymph nodes; followed by skin grafting. This is rarely done nowadays.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="chemotherapy">Chemotherapy<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#chemotherapy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="radiation-therapy">Radiation Therapy<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#radiation-therapy" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="care-of-clients-with-breast-cancer">CARE OF CLIENTS WITH BREAST CANCER<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#care-of-clients-with-breast-cancer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client undergoing breast surgery</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-68660dfe.jpeg" alt="img-107.jpeg"></p>
<p>PREOPERATIVE CARE</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>PROCEDURE</th><th>RATIONALE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Psychosocial Support. Include the husband when necessary.</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Teach arm exercises</td><td>to prevent lymph edema</td></tr><tr><td>Inform about wound suction drainage (hemovac, Jackson-Pratt)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>DBCT exercises</td><td>to prevent postop respiratory complications</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client undergoing breast surgery</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-fd878931.jpeg" alt="img-108.jpeg"></p>
<p>POSTOPERATIVE CARE</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>PROCEDURE</th><th>RATIONALE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Place client in semi-Fowler's position with arm abducted and elevated on pillows.</td><td>- position promotes lung expansion</td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul>
<li>abduction and elevation of am on the affected side promotes venous return and prevents lymphedema  |
|  Monitor Hemovac output | - normal drainage is serosanguinous (first 24 hours)</li>
<li>composed of plasma and small amounts of RBC, pinkish or reddish in appearance but not viscous  |</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client undergoing breast surgery</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-fec98781.jpeg" alt="img-109.jpeg"></p>
<p>POSTOPERATIVE CARE</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>PROCEDURE</th><th>RATIONALE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Check behind patient for bleeding</td><td>Blood flows to the back by gravity.</td></tr><tr><td>Post signs warning against taking blood pressure, starting IVs, or drawing blood on affected side.</td><td>to prevent obstruction of venous and lymphatic flow.</td></tr><tr><td>Initiate exercise. Give analgesic before initiating exercises</td><td>to prevent stiffness and contractures of shoulder girdle</td></tr><tr><td>Reinforce special mastectomy exercises as prescribed</td><td>to prevent lymphedema</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client undergoing breast surgery</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-1e75c752.jpeg" alt="img-110.jpeg"></p>
<p>POSTOPERATIVE CARE</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>PROCEDURE</th><th>RATIONALE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Provide adequate analgesia to promote ambulation and exercise</td><td>The client cooperates with ambulation and exercise if she is free from pain or discomfort</td></tr><tr><td>Encourage regular coughing and deep breathing exercises</td><td>to promote lung expansion and prevent atelectasis</td></tr><tr><td>Prepare client for size and appearance of the incision and provide support when incision is viewed for first time.</td><td></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client undergoing breast surgery</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-71973ce3.jpeg" alt="img-111.jpeg"></p>
<p>POSTOPERATIVE CARE</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>PROCEDURE</th><th>RATIONALE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Provide client with detailed information concerning breast prosthesis.</td><td>Fitting is not possible for 4 - 6 wks. A temporary prosthesis or lightly paddled bras may be worn until healing is complete.</td></tr><tr><td>Teach patient to avoid constrictive clothing and report persistent edera, redness, or infection of incision.</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Teach patient importance of continuing monthly breast examination remaining breast.</td><td></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-5a044dc2.jpeg" alt="img-112.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="assessment-findings">ASSESSMENT FINDINGS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#assessment-findings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>ascending (right) colon: occult blood in stool, anemia, anorexia and weight loss, abdominal above umbilicus, palpable mass</li>
<li>distal colon and rectum: hematochezia, alternating constipation and diarrhea, pencil or ribbon-shaped stool, pain below umbilicus</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="collaborative-management">COLLABORATIVE MANAGEMENT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#collaborative-management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>surgery:</li>
<li>Hemicolectomy - ascending and transverse colon</li>
<li>Abdominoperineal resection (Mile’s Surgery) - rectosigmoid colon</li>
<li>involves 2 incisions: lower abdominal (sigmoid removal); perineal (rectum removal)</li>
<li>requires permanent colostomy</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="care-of-clients-with-colorectal-cancer">CARE OF CLIENTS WITH COLORECTAL CANCER<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#care-of-clients-with-colorectal-cancer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client undergoing colonic surgery</p>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="preoperative-care">PREOPERATIVE CARE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#preoperative-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<table><thead><tr><th>NURSING CARE</th><th>PROCEDURE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Provide psychological support</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Promotion of thorough bowel cleaning</td><td>- diet modification:</td></tr></tbody></table>
<blockquote>
<p>low residue diet 3-5 days preop (to reduce bulk of feces)
clear liquid diet 24 hours preop</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>mechanical cleansing:</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>laxative as ordered
cleansing enema or intestinal evacuant as ordered</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>neomycin SO4 tablets  |</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client undergoing colonic surgery</p>

<p>PREOPERATIVE CARE</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>NURSING CARE</th><th>PROCEDURE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Risk for infection and bleeding</td><td>- administer vit C and K as ordered (these are lost in repeated enema)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions">NURSING INTERVENTIONS:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>client undergoing colonic surgery</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-7ff5e11b.jpeg" alt="img-115.jpeg"></p>
<p>POSTOPERATIVE CARE</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>NURSING CARE</th><th>PROCEDURE</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Managing perineal wound in APR</td><td>- warm sitz bath to promote healing and relieve pain</td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul>
<li>side lying position during sleep to prevent pressure and pain  |
|  Stoma monitoring | - check for signs of ischemia and necrosis</li>
<li>check for prolapse stoma</li>
<li>flatus and fecal drainage begin in 4-7 days</li>
<li>colostomy care  |
|  Patient independence | - health teaching  |</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-5a044dc2.jpeg" alt="img-116.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="assessment-findings">ASSESSMENT FINDINGS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#assessment-findings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>most characteristic manifestation is painless hematuria</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="collaborative-management">COLLABORATIVE MANAGEMENT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#collaborative-management" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>surgery: urinary diversions (after removal of bladder)</li>
<li>Ileal conduit – ureters are implanted into a segment of ileum</li>
<li>Koch pouch – pouch created from a segment of ileum, ureters are implanted into the side of the pouch; client inserts straight catheter q 4-6 hours</li>
<li>Indiana pouch – a continent reservoir created from the ascending colon and terminal ileum; larger than Koch pouch; straight catheter q 4-6 hours</li>
<li>Ureterostomy – ureters are attached to the surface of abdomen</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="care-of-clients-with-bladder-cancer">CARE OF CLIENTS WITH BLADDER CANCER<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#care-of-clients-with-bladder-cancer" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251227-5fa0e174.jpeg" alt="img-117.jpeg"></p>
<ul>
<li>Vesicostomy – bladder is sutured to the abdomen, and stoma is created in the bladder wall</li>
<li>Percutaneous nephrostomy – insertion of a tube into the kidney for drainage; done if the cancer is inoperable</li>
</ul>
<p>CARE OF CLIENTS WITH BLADDER CANCER</p>
<p>-End-</p>
